| Ingest | ‡∏î‡∏∂‡∏á CSV / API / DB  |
| Transform | clean, normalize, join  |
| Model | fact / dimension  |
| Define metric | ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô `satisfaction_score`  |
| Data contract | ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢ + rule  |
| Quality | null, outlier, logic  |
| Access | ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏Ñ‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏∑‡πà‡∏ô query ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ  |

> ‡∏à‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏à‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏∑‡∏≠:  
> **‚Äú‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤ analyst ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô SELECT ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ = ‡∏à‡∏ö‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô DE‚Äù**

## ‡∏ä‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà 1: Data Minimalism Layer (‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î)

> ‚Äú‡∏ó‡∏≥‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ AI ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏≤‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‚Äù

### ‡∏™‡∏¥‡πà‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏£‡∏°‡∏µ (‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏û‡∏≠)

## ‡∏ä‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà 2: Metric & Question Contract

‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å ‚Äú‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏° AI ‡∏≠‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏£‡∏Å‡πá‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‚Äù

## Skill ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì ‚Äú‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏£‡∏°‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‚Äù (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà Data Engineer ‡πÄ‡∏ï‡πá‡∏°‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß)

## Workflow ‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà (‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏¥‡∏° + ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏° 30%)

## Master Prompt: AI Data Steward Audit

‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏á prompt ‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ _‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å_ Claude Code ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏´‡πå‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏£‡πá‡∏à‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß

---

### üîç Prompt ‡∏ä‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å (‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏ô‡∏≥‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Å‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ô)

## 2Ô∏è‚É£ `metrics.yaml`

> üëâ ‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏©‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á ‚Äú‡∏Ñ‡∏ô ‚Äì AI ‚Äì ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏£‚Äù

`satisfaction_avg:   description: ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏û‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏û‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏à‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏°   calc: mean(satisfaction)  low_satisfaction_ratio:   description: ‡∏™‡∏±‡∏î‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏Ñ‡∏∞‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≥ (<=2)   calc: count(satisfaction<=2)/count(*)  fairness_avg:   description: ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ‡∏™‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏ò‡∏£‡∏£‡∏°   calc: mean(fairness)  process_issue_mentions:   description: ‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Å‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ß‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£   source: comment   method: text classification  role_gap_satisfaction:   description: ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÅ‡∏ï‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏û‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏û‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏à‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏ó   calc: mean(satisfaction) grouped by role`

üìå **‡∏Å‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏≤:**

## 4Ô∏è‚É£ `ai_data_audit.md` (Generated by AI ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á)

## üß† Workflow ‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà (‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏î ‡πÜ)

## ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÇ‡∏¢‡∏Ñ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏£‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏¢‡∏∂‡∏î

> ‚ÄúAI ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡πå‡∏Ñ‡∏¥‡∏î  
> ‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡πå‡∏Ñ‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‚Äù

‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏Ç‡∏≤‡∏î skill  
‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì‡πÅ‡∏Ñ‡πà **‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏° skill ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á AI**

‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏Å:

-   ‡∏ó‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô **template repo**
    
-   ‡πÅ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô **docker compose**
    
-   ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô **AI Survey Brain (‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ MCP)**

## STEP 1 ‚Äî Data ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏π‡πà Framework (‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô Steward)

üìå ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ‡∏Ñ‡∏∑‡∏≠ ‚Äú‡∏≠‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏©‡∏¢‡πå‚Äù

## 2Ô∏è‚É£ MCP Spec (Survey Brain Edition)

### MCP Roles

yaml

`roles:   - name: survey_data_steward     responsibility:       - inspect_schema       - assess_quality       - detect_bias       - document_assumptions    - name: survey_analyst     responsibility:       - derive_metrics       - pattern_detection       - segment_analysis    - name: insight_facilitator     responsibility:       - role_based_prompting       - narrative_synthesis       - recommendation_framing`

üëâ **1 LLM ‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô ‚Äú‡∏´‡∏°‡∏ß‡∏Å‚Äù ‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô MCP**

---

### MCP State Flow

text

`RAW_DATA   ‚Üì PROFILED_DATA   ‚Üì CURATED_DATA   ‚Üì ANALYSIS_READY   ‚Üì ROLE_BASED_INSIGHT   ‚Üì AUDITED_OUTPUT`

**‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å state = file + explanation**  
‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ ‚Äú‡∏Ñ‡∏¥‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏¢ ‡πÜ‚Äù

---

## 3Ô∏è‚É£ MCP Tool List (‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏Å)

‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏∑‡∏≠ **Tool ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà AI ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏ó‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ**

### Core Tools

yaml

`tools:   inspect_dataset:     input: csv_path     output:       - schema       - row_count       - missing_rate       - data_types    quality_check:     input: csv_path     output:       - missing_values       - inconsistent_labels       - outliers    bias_scan:     input: csv_path     output:       - skewed_questions       - response_distribution       - sample_warning    build_embeddings:     input: text_columns     output:       - vector_store_path    rag_query:     input:       - question       - role     output:       - cited_chunks       - confidence_level    generate_report:     input:       - role       - insights     output:       - markdown_report`

üëâ ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ tool = AI ‡∏ó‡∏≥‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ  
üëâ ‡∏°‡∏µ tool = ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á log ‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏£

---

## 4Ô∏è‚É£ Docker Compose Architecture (Local PoC ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏ñ‡∏ô‡∏±‡∏î)

### ‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏°

text

`[ CSV / Survey Data ]         |         v [ survey-loader ]         |         v [ MCP Server ] ----> [ Vector DB ]         |         v [ Local LLM (Ollama / LM Studio) ]`

---

### docker-compose.yml (conceptual)

yaml

`version: "3.9"  services:   llm:     image: ollama/ollama     volumes:       - ollama:/root/.ollama     ports:       - "11434:11434"    vectorstore:     image: qdrant/qdrant     ports:       - "6333:6333"    mcp-server:     build: ./mcp-server     volumes:       - ./data:/data       - ./reports:/reports     environment:       - LLM_ENDPOINT=http://llm:11434       - VECTOR_DB=http://vectorstore:6333     depends_on:       - llm       - vectorstore    survey-ui:     build: ./ui     ports:       - "8501:8501"     depends_on:       - mcp-server  volumes:   ollama:`

---

## ‡∏ñ‡∏±‡∏î‡πÑ‡∏õ (‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÇ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏Å)

3 ‡∏Å‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ß‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡πâ‡∏°:

-   AI ‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏Å ‚Äú‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‚Äù ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ

> üß† ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ñ‡∏ô‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤

> **‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏° Level** (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏á‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏õ‡∏ß‡∏î‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏Å)

## üß† AI Survey Brain ‚Äì Prompt Pack by Level

---

## üü£ Level 1 ‚Äî Survey-Aware AI

### ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≤: _AI ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô_

### Prompt: Dataset Inspection

text

`You are a Survey Data Inspector.  Task: 1. Describe the dataset structure. 2. List all columns with inferred data types. 3. Count total responses. 4. Identify open-ended vs closed-ended questions.  Rules: - Do NOT analyze sentiment or draw insights. - Do NOT summarize results. - If any information is unclear, state it explicitly.  Output: Write to dataset_profile.md`

---

## üü£ Level 2 ‚Äî AI Data Steward

### ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≤: _AI ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•_

### Prompt: Data Quality & Bias Audit

text

`You are an AI Data Steward.  Before any analysis: 1. State all assumptions you must make. 2. Identify missing or inconsistent data. 3. Detect potential bias or sampling issues. 4. List what cannot be concluded from this dataset.  Rules: - Do NOT provide insights or recommendations. - Use cautious, professional language. - Explicitly label uncertainty.  Output: Write to ai_data_audit.md`

---

## üü† Level 3 ‚Äî Role-Based Insight Engine

### ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≤: _AI ‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô_

---

### Prompt A: Executive Insight

text

`Role: Insight Facilitator Audience: Executive Committee  Context: - Dataset has passed quality and bias checks. - Assumptions are documented.  Task: 1. Provide up to 5 strategic insights. 2. Each insight must cite specific data evidence. 3. Include one uncertainty or risk per insight.  Rules: - Focus on decisions, not methodology. - Avoid technical jargon.  Output: markdown report (executive_summary.md)`

---

### Prompt B: Working Team Insight

text

`Role: Survey Analyst Audience: Field Operations Team  Task: 1. Identify operational issues and strengths. 2. Reference exact survey questions where relevant. 3. Suggest practical follow-up actions.  Rules: - Do not generalize beyond the data. - Flag any low-confidence findings.  Output: markdown report (team_insights.md)`

---

### Prompt C: Participant Feedback

text

`Role: Insight Facilitator Audience: Survey Participants  Task: 1. Summarize overall feedback themes. 2. Highlight what will be improved. 3. Acknowledge limitations of the survey.  Rules: - Use respectful and transparent language. - Avoid internal or sensitive findings.  Output: markdown report (participant_summary.md)`

---

## üî¥ Level 4 ‚Äî Survey Memory (Cross-Survey)

### Prompt: Cross-Survey Comparison

text

`Role: Survey Memory Curator  Task: 1. Compare the current survey with previous surveys. 2. Identify stable themes vs changing themes. 3. Explicitly state which questions or results are NOT comparable. 4. Describe observed trends only when supported by at least two surveys.  Rules: - Do NOT force comparisons. - Clearly label confidence level for each trend. - Avoid narrative exaggeration.  Output: markdown report (cross_survey_trends.md)`

---

## üî¥ Level 4+ ‚Äî Insight Registration (Memory Update)

text

`Role: Survey Memory Curator  Task: 1. Review newly generated insights. 2. Select only insights with confidence ‚â• 0.6. 3. Store each insight with:    - theme    - evidence surveys    - uncertainty notes 4. Reject any insight that is redundant or weakly supported.  Rules: - Memory is curated, not exhaustive. - Document rejected insights with reasons.  Output: update insight_memory.yaml`

---

## üß† Universal Emergency Prompt (‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏´‡∏•‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á)

text

`Before proceeding, explain: 1. What data you have used. 2. What assumptions you are making. 3. What you are NOT doing yet. 4. What the next safe step is.  If any step is unclear, stop and ask for clarification.`

---

## üéØ ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ò‡∏µ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á (‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏ô‡∏≥‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏Å)

-   1 survey run =  
    Level 1 ‚Üí Level 2 ‚Üí Level 3 ‚Üí (‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏µ) Level 4
    
-   **‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°** ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏° AI ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á ‡πÜ
    
-   ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å output ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà‡πÅ‡∏Ñ‡πà chat)
    

---

## ‡∏ñ‡∏±‡∏î‡πÑ‡∏õ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏ö‡∏≤ ‡πÜ (‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á)

‡∏ú‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏≥‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏Å:

1.  üì¶ Prompt pack ‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô **repo structure**
    
2.  üß™ Example data + expected output
    
3.  üß© Prompt ‚Üí MCP tool mapping
    

‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏°‡∏≤ 1 ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ô  
‡∏™‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ç‡∏≤‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏®‡∏±‡∏û‡∏ó‡πå‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß üòÇ

##### You said:

Prompt ‚Üí MCP tool mapping

###### ChatGPT said:

‡∏°‡∏≤ ‡πÜ ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ‡∏Ñ‡∏∑‡∏≠ **‡∏à‡∏¥‡πä‡∏Å‡∏ã‡∏≠‡∏ß‡πå‡∏ä‡∏¥‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏ó‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ó‡∏≥‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ ‚Äúprompt ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏¢‚Äù** üß©  
‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡πã‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏ú‡∏°‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö **‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤ prompt ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏ô ‚Üí ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏Å MCP tool ‡∏≠‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏£ ‚Üí ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ artifact ‡∏≠‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏£**  
‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ‡∏™‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤ _‚Äú‡∏≠‡πã‡∏≠‚Ä¶ ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏´‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏õ‡∏ß‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ mapping ‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á‚Äù_ üòÑ

---

## üîå Prompt ‚Üí MCP Tool Mapping (AI Survey Brain)

> ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏¥‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏ç‡πà  
> **Prompt = ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏à**  
> **Tool = ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á**  
> **File = ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô**

‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤ prompt ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏ô **‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ú‡∏π‡∏Å tool** ‚Üí ‡∏ô‡∏±‡πà‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏∑‡∏≠ hallucination risk

---

## üü£ Level 1 ‚Äî Survey-Aware AI

### ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≤: ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô

### Prompt

**Dataset Inspection**

text

`Describe dataset structure, columns, and response count. Do NOT analyze or summarize.`

### MCP Tool Mapping

| ‡∏•‡∏≥‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö | MCP Tool | ‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏≠‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏£  |
--- | --- | ---

| 1 | `inspect_dataset` | ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô schema / row count  |
| 2 | `classify_questions` | ‡πÅ‡∏¢‡∏Å open-ended / closed  |
| 3 | `export_profile` | ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô dataset\_profile.md  |

### Output Artifacts

-   `dataset_profile.md`
    

üëâ ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ = **‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô Level 1**

---

## üü£ Level 2 ‚Äî AI Data Steward

### ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≤: ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•

### Prompt

**Data Quality & Bias Audit**

text

`State assumptions, detect bias, list limitations. Do NOT generate insights.`

### MCP Tool Mapping

| ‡∏•‡∏≥‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö | MCP Tool | ‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏≠‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏£  |
--- | --- | ---

| 1 | `quality_check` | missing / inconsistency  |
| 2 | `bias_scan` | distribution / skew  |
